<script>
    // Removes query params from url
    if ("undefined" !== typeof history.replaceState && 'undefined' !== typeof URL) {
        let newUrl = new URL(window.location.href);
        let paramsToRemove = [
            'store_token',
            'cart_token',
            'gift',
            'clearCart',
            'redirectTo',
            'product_option_id',
            'quantity',
            'metadata',
            'has_recomm',
            'kit_id',
            'isShopify',
            'customerToken',
            'addressId',
        ].join('|');

        let regex = new RegExp(`[?|&](?:${paramsToRemove})(?:\[[a-z0-9_-]+\]|\[\])?=([^?&]*)`, 'g');
        let urlParams =  decodeURIComponent(newUrl.search).replace(regex, '');

        if (urlParams.length && urlParams.startsWith('&')) {
            urlParams = '?'+ urlParams.substring(1);
        }

        let finalUrl = newUrl.origin + newUrl.pathname + urlParams;

        if (window.location.href !== finalUrl) {
            history.replaceState({}, null, finalUrl);
        }
    }
</script>

<script>
    // Removes query params from url
    if ("undefined" !== typeof history.replaceState && 'undefined' !== typeof URL) {
        let newUrl = new URL(window.location.href);
        let paramsToRemove = [
            'store_token',
            'cart_token',
            'gift',
            'clearCart',
            'redirectTo',
            'product_option_id',
            'quantity',
            'metadata',
            'has_recomm',
            'kit_id',
            'isShopify',
            'customerToken',
            'addressId',
        ].join('|');

        let regex = new RegExp(`[?|&](?:${paramsToRemove})(?:\[[a-z0-9_-]+\]|\[\])?=([^?&]*)`, 'g');
        let urlParams =  decodeURIComponent(newUrl.search).replace(regex, '');

        if (urlParams.length && urlParams.startsWith('&')) {
            urlParams = '?'+ urlParams.substring(1);
        }

        let finalUrl = newUrl.origin + newUrl.pathname + urlParams;

        if (window.location.href !== finalUrl) {
            history.replaceState({}, null, finalUrl);
        }
    }
</script>

<script>
    // Removes query params from url
    if ("undefined" !== typeof history.replaceState && 'undefined' !== typeof URL) {
        let newUrl = new URL(window.location.href);
        let paramsToRemove = [
            'store_token',
            'cart_token',
            'gift',
            'clearCart',
            'redirectTo',
            'product_option_id',
            'quantity',
            'metadata',
            'has_recomm',
            'kit_id',
            'isShopify',
            'customerToken',
            'addressId',
        ].join('|');

        let regex = new RegExp(`[?|&](?:${paramsToRemove})(?:\[[a-z0-9_-]+\]|\[\])?=([^?&]*)`, 'g');
        let urlParams =  decodeURIComponent(newUrl.search).replace(regex, '');

        if (urlParams.length && urlParams.startsWith('&')) {
            urlParams = '?'+ urlParams.substring(1);
        }

        let finalUrl = newUrl.origin + newUrl.pathname + urlParams;

        if (window.location.href !== finalUrl) {
            history.replaceState({}, null, finalUrl);
        }
    }
</script>

<script>
    // Removes query params from url
    if ("undefined" !== typeof history.replaceState && 'undefined' !== typeof URL) {
        let newUrl = new URL(window.location.href);
        let paramsToRemove = [
            'store_token',
            'cart_token',
            'gift',
            'clearCart',
            'redirectTo',
            'product_option_id',
            'quantity',
            'metadata',
            'has_recomm',
            'kit_id',
            'isShopify',
            'customerToken',
            'addressId',
        ].join('|');

        let regex = new RegExp(`[?|&](?:${paramsToRemove})(?:\[[a-z0-9_-]+\]|\[\])?=([^?&]*)`, 'g');
        let urlParams =  decodeURIComponent(newUrl.search).replace(regex, '');

        if (urlParams.length && urlParams.startsWith('&')) {
            urlParams = '?'+ urlParams.substring(1);
        }

        let finalUrl = newUrl.origin + newUrl.pathname + urlParams;

        if (window.location.href !== finalUrl) {
            history.replaceState({}, null, finalUrl);
        }
    }
</script>

<script>
    // Removes query params from url
    if ("undefined" !== typeof history.replaceState && 'undefined' !== typeof URL) {
        let newUrl = new URL(window.location.href);
        let paramsToRemove = [
            'store_token',
            'cart_token',
            'gift',
            'clearCart',
            'redirectTo',
            'product_option_id',
            'quantity',
            'metadata',
            'has_recomm',
            'kit_id',
            'isShopify',
            'customerToken',
            'addressId',
        ].join('|');

        let regex = new RegExp(`[?|&](?:${paramsToRemove})(?:\[[a-z0-9_-]+\]|\[\])?=([^?&]*)`, 'g');
        let urlParams =  decodeURIComponent(newUrl.search).replace(regex, '');

        if (urlParams.length && urlParams.startsWith('&')) {
            urlParams = '?'+ urlParams.substring(1);
        }

        let finalUrl = newUrl.origin + newUrl.pathname + urlParams;

        if (window.location.href !== finalUrl) {
            history.replaceState({}, null, finalUrl);
        }
    }
</script>
